< Text>
I had a storage unit here for a few months (temporary move) and this place was great. It was an easy process to get the unit, I actually reserved it online and was able to walk in on move-in day to purchase a lock & was shown the unit within minutes. Every one of the staff I dealt w/ while coming into the office was great and pleasant to work with. They seem to monitor the grounds frequently. I moved out in a rush before the office had opened so I couldn't close my account right then but when I called to close it, they advised they had already seen it was empty and closed out my account, which I appreciate so much. If you need a storage unit, long term or short, this is definitely the place to go. It's also super convenient w/ Dunkin next door! Pre-move fuel lol Thank you Orangecrest Self Storage! I will definitely consider you guys again if I ever need to move out this way again.</Text>

<UserId.>106918382879011329321</UserId.>< user_name>
Kevin Mcnamee<//user_name>
<date>1619673226450<//date><rate>5<//rate>< Review>
I did a 7.2 mile loop here on April 10, 2021, you can see my trail recording on the Alltrails app, just look up my name and please follow me for more fun trails and my reviews.

This is a busy place to hike, but it has a lot of different trails to explore. The views are really nice, you can see the ocean from many spots. The entire place is very clean and kudos to what ever dept cares for this land. If you really want to get a great workout in, make your way to the Poles Trail. This is a leg burner, but worth it. There are also plenty of nice shady canyon trails you can take if you want to stay out of the sun. There are so many trails, I'll have to go back to explore more.

If you are interested in joining in any hikes, you can find my hikes on the "Meet Up" app under the group "Five Miles or More Hiking Group" with the times and places I'll be going. Enjoy your hiking.< /Review>

< review>
Can't say anything bad about this trail head. Have multiple hiking trail, trail are pretty well maintain and have incline when it there. You will have a pretty work out on this trail. Can also get crowded too on the weekend. It my first time here and when I went there it was pretty foggy in the morning so didn't get to see my surrounding. Also, there no tree for shade so go early n if you do go during the afternoon please bring lots of water. They allow bike here on the trail so be careful because they came fast.< /review>

We are new to El Segundo and have been trying the local Japanese restaurants, as that is our favorite cuisine. We ordered an assortment of dishes and took them home to eat. <time>1589208191326< /time>< Text>
Outstanding and quality educational experience and training. If you are in Healthcare and need to update your certifications, THIS IS A GREAT PLACE to get your refreshers and on the spot CEU's.

If you want to be one certified and are getting into the health care system,  THIS IS THE PLACE.

California Medical Training uses a great concept of hybrid learning.  They use a pre-course  online syllabus, you get to take practice quizzes and practice test, which PREPARES YOU for the 1st day of class to the completion of class.

This concept makes you a success and helps you better understand the information which you have a great learning experience and gives you a high passing rate.

During the in class experience, the instructors are extremely passionate about their teaching and they are well versed on the latest trends in the course they teach.

They also use high quality videos, worksheets, and have the hands on equipment to cement the learning process and you, as a student, end up with really high scores.

Lastly, the instructors work with you on a 1 to 1 for clarification, explanations and demonstrations, before,  during and after class as well as via texts and emails.

Also, your certificates are READY at the end of the course or temporary certificates are provided until you get the official certificate from the issuing agency, depending on your course.

Overall I have taken 3 classes with California Medical Training and never have been disappointed. Also, the price for these classes are much more affordable and below the current rate as compared to other training programs.

These instructors have a vested interest in their students and in their success with their Healthcare Educational Goals.<//Text>

<Review>I traveled from Florida to Los Angeles, California to take three specific courses from California Medical Training Center: trach/vent, ABG interpretation, and airway management/modes of oxygenation. The trip was well worth it!!! All three courses were fantastic. The knowledge I gained from these courses has helped me tremendously in my job. I work as a speech-language pathologist in a hospital, where most of my patients have a tracheostomy tube in place and/or require ventilatory support. I needed formal instruction from an experienced respiratory therapist in order to better serve my patients with voicing and swallowing difficulties.  I didn't feel that these patients deserved to be neglected just because of my incompetence. So I signed up for these courses and flew across the state! Justin was my instructor for all three courses and was an excellent teacher. He's got a wealth of hands-on clinical experience and is very personable!!!! Mike, the owner, was also incredibly helpful and informative! I appreciated the time he took to share his clinical knowledge and expertise on speaking valves for trach/vent patients.Two weeks ago, I was able to safely place my first in-line speaking valve on a spinal cord injury patient requiring vent support. Because of this in-line speaking valve placement/trial, the patient had the opportunity to have a conversation with their kids for the first time in multiple months. Thankfully, this patient has been tolerating the in-line speaking valve during my therapy sessions with them over the past few weeks. And when the alarms sounded during placement and tracheo-bronchial suctioning, I knew how to troubleshoot! I also have many other trach/vent patients that are being seen sooner during their hospital stay due to knowledge Justin shared with me during the three courses. Thanks so much to California Medical Training Center for providing me with a wealth of much-needed trach/vent/pulmonary knowledge to help  better serve my patients with a tracheostomy tube and/or ventilator.</Review>< Pictures>
